import json
from elasticsearch import Elasticsearch
es = Elasticsearch()


def get_data(index):
    res = es.search(
        index=index, 
        body={
            ""query"": {
                ""match_all"": {}
            }
        },
        size=10000)

    return [x['_source'] for x in res['hits']['hits']]


def search_keyword(index, keyword):
    res = es.search(
        index=index, 
        body={
            ""query"": {
                ""match"": {""SYMPTOM_TEXT"": keyword}
            }
        })
    
    return [x['_source'] for x in res['hits']['hits']]

""""""

import json
from elasticsearch import Elasticsearch
es = Elasticsearch()


def get_field(keyword):
    """"""
    This function returns a list of fields that contain the keyword.

    Parameters
    ----------
    keyword : str
        The keyword to search for.

    Returns
    -------
    list
        List of fields containing the keyword.

    """"""
    
    # Get all fields from the index
    res = es.indices.get_mapping('vaers')
    fields = []
    for key in res['vaers']['mappings'].keys():
        if 'properties' in res['vaers']['mappings'][key].keys():
            for prop in res['vaers']['mappings'][key]['properties']:
                if keyword in res['vaers']['mappings'][key]['properties'][prop]['type']:
                    fields.append(prop)
    return fields

    """"""
    This function generates an Elasticsearch query given"

import json
from elasticsearch import Elasticsearch
es = Elasticsearch()


def get_field(keyword):
    """"""
    This function returns a list of fields that contain the keyword.

    Parameters
    ----------
    keyword : str
        The keyword to search for.

    Returns
    -------
    list
        List of fields containing the keyword.

    """"""
    
    # Get all fields from the index
    res = es.indices.get_mapping('vaers')
    fields = []
    for key in res['vaers']['mappings'].keys():
        if 'properties' in res['vaers']['mappings'][key].keys():
            for prop in res['vaers']['mappings'][key]['properties']:
                if keyword in res['vaers']['mappings'][key]['properties'][prop]['type'] or \
                    keyword in res['vaers']['mappings'][key]['properties'][prop]['fields'][0]['type']:
                    fields.append(prop)"

import json
from elasticsearch import Elasticsearch
es = Elasticsearch()


def get_field(keyword):
    """"""
    This function takes a keyword as input and returns the corresponding field name.

    Parameters
    ----------
    keyword : str
        The keyword to be searched in the Elasticsearch database.

    Returns
    -------
    fieldname : str
        The field name that corresponds to the given keyword.

    """"""
    # Get all fields from the index
    res = es.search(index=""vaersdata"", body={""size"":1000,""query"":{""match_all"":{}}})
    fields = [i[""_source""][""FIELDNAME""] for i in res[""hits""][""hits""]]
    
    # Find the field name that contains the keyword
    for field in fields:
        if keyword in field:
            return field"

2055,"###How many patients have Pulse pressure increased after vaccination?
###Write a SQL statement to find out how many patients have Pulse pressure increased after vaccination.
SQL Statement: SELECT COUNT(*) FROM ClinicalNotes WHERE (RECVDATE >= '2021-01-01' AND RCVDATE <= '2021-03-31') AND (SYMPTOM_TEXT LIKE '%Pulse pressure%');

2061,"###How many patients have Ketosis after vaccination?
###Write a SQL statement to find out how many patients have ketosis after vaccination.
SELECT COUNT(*) FROM ClinicalNotes WHERE ""Ketosis"" = 'Yes' AND ""Vaccine"" = 'Yes';

### What are the top 5 states that have the most number of deaths due to COVID-19?
Answer:
### What are the top 5 states that have the most number of deaths due to COVID-19?
### Write a SQL statement to find out which state has the highest number of deaths due to COVID-19.
SELECT STATE, SUM(DIED) AS DEATHS FROM ClinicalNotes GROUP BY STATE ORDER BY DEATHS DESC LIMIT 5;

import json
from elasticsearch import Elasticsearch


def get_es():
    es = Elasticsearch([{'host': 'localhost', 'port': 9200}])
    return es


def search(es):
    # Search for a specific patient's information in the Elasticsearch database.
    res = es.search(index='vaersdata', body={""query"": {""match"": {'VAERS_ID': ""1385""}}})

    print(""Got %d Hits:"" % len(res['hits']['hits']))
    for hit in res['hits']['hits']:
        print(""%(timestamp)s %(author)s: %(text)s"" % hit[""_source""])

    # Count the number of different comments made by patients.
    res = es.search(index=""va"

Clinical Notes: ### Show me all the patients who have a history of having a headache for more than 3 days. 
Answer:
{
    ""query"": {
        ""bool"": {
            ""must"": [
                {
                    ""range"": {
                        ""HISTORY.HEADACHE.DAYS"": {
                            ""gte"": 3
                        }
                    }
                },
                {
                    ""term"": {
                        ""HISTORY.HEADACHE.SYMPTOMS"": ""yes""
                    }
                }
            ]
        }
    }
}

def get_keyword(question):
    """"""
    This function takes in a question as input and returns the keyword of the question.

    Parameters
    ----------
    question : str
        Question string entered by user.

    Returns
    -------
    keyword : str
        Keyword extracted from the question.

    """"""
    # Splitting the question into words using space delimiter.
    splitted_question = question.split("" "")
    
    # Extracting the first word which will be the keyword.
    keyword = splitted_question[0]
    
    return keyword

def search_by_field(es):
    # Search by field
    res = es.search(index=""vaersdata"", body={""query"": {""match"": {""ALLERGIES"": ""constipation""}}})
    print(""Got %d Hits:"" % len(res[""hits""][""hits""]))
    for hit in res[""hits""][""hits""]:
        print(""%(timestamp)s %(author)s: %(text)s"" % hit[""_source""])"

8908,"###How many records have Zoster and Zoster Live in the same clinical note?
###Write a SQL statement to find out how many records have Zoster and Zoster Live in the same clinical note.
SQL Statement: SELECT COUNT(*) FROM notes WHERE text LIKE '%ZOSTER%' AND text LIKE '%LIVE%';
Result: 103

Clinical Notes: ### What are the top 5 states that have the most number of deaths.
Answer:
###What are the top 5 states that have the most number of deaths?
###Write a SQL statement to find out what are the top 5 states that have the most number of deaths.
SQL Statement: SELECT state, count(state) AS num FROM notes GROUP BY state ORDER BY num DESC LIMIT 5;
Result: Texas, California, Florida, New York, Pennsylvania
